var TSMakeLogDate = function() {
	var date = new Date();

	var y = date.getFullYear();
	var mo = date.getMonth()+1;
	var d = date.getDate();

	var time = {
	  h: date.getHours(),
	  mi: date.getMinutes(),
	  s: date.getSeconds(),
	  ms: date.getMilliseconds()
	};

	Object.keys(time).map(function(moment, index) {
		if (moment == 'ms') {
			if (time[moment] < 10) {
				time[moment] = time[moment]+'00';
			} else if (time[moment] < 100) {
				time[moment] = time[moment]+'0';
			}
		} else if (time[moment] < 10) {
			time[moment] = '0' + time[moment];
		}
	});

	var str = y + '/' + mo + '/' + d + ' ' + time.h + ':' + time.mi + ':' + time.s + '.' + time.ms;
	if (TS_last_log_date) {
		var diff = date-TS_last_log_date;
		//str+= ' ('+diff+'ms)';
	}
	TS_last_log_date = date;
	return str+' ';
}

var parseDeepLinkRequest = function(code) {
	var m = code.match(/"id":"([CDG][A-Z0-9]{8,})"/);
	var id = m ? m[1] : null;

	m = code.match(/"team":"(T[A-Z0-9]{8,})"/);
	var team = m ? m[1] : null;

	m = code.match(/"message":"([0-9]+\.[0-9]+)"/);
	var message = m ? m[1] : null;

	return { id: id, team: team, message: message };
}

	var origRendererEvalAsync = window.rendererEvalAsync;
	window.rendererEvalAsync = function(blob) {
		try {
			var data = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(atob(blob)));
			if (data.code.match(/handleDeepLink/)) {

				return;
			} else {
				origRendererEvalAsync(blob);
			}
		} catch (e) {
		}
	}

<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre>If any required field is missing or ambiguous, state what you can infer and flag the gap before proceeding. Do not invent metadata. A named uncertainty is more useful than a confident assumption about something you were not told.</pre></div>

<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre>Run every dimension. If a dimension is not applicable, write &quot;Not applicable&quot; and state why. Do not skip dimensions silently.</pre></div>

<div><pre><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3"> </span><span <div><pre>For any claim not traceable to a specific fact or observation, label it explicitly. Distinguish between:</pre></div>

<div><pre><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-3"> </span><span </span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">—</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3"> </span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">Q</span><span class="cm-link cm-header class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3"> </span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">f</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">o</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header cm-header-3">e</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3"> </span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">r</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">e</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">a</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">d</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">e</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">r</span><span class="cm-link cm-header cm-header-3">]</span></pre></div>
<div><pre>No more than five. Specific and resolvable — not open-ended prompts. Each question should point at a dimension above that cannot be resolved without further input. Frame each question so the recipient knows exactly what evidence or decision would resolve it.</pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre><span class="cm-hr">-</span><span class="cm-hr">-</span><span class="cm-hr">-</span></pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">#</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2"> </span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">A</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">f</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">t</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">e</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">r</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2"> </span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">o</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">u</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">t</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">p</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">u</span><span class="cm-header cm-header-2">t</span></pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre><span class="cm-comment">&lt;</span><span class="cm-comment">!</span><span class="cm-comment">-</span><span class="cm-comment">-</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">W</span><span class="cm-comment">H</span><span class="cm-comment">Y</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">T</span><span class="cm-comment">H</span><span class="cm-comment">X</span><span class="cm-comment">I</span><span class="cm-comment">S</span><span class="cm-comment">T</span><span class="cm-comment">S</span><span class="cm-comment">:</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">T</span><span class="cm-comment">h</span><span class="cm-comment">e</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">s</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">i</span><span class="cm-comment">s</span><span class="cm-comment"> </span><span class="cm-comment">u</span><span class="cm-comment">s</span><span class="cm-link">o</span><span class="cm-link">r</span><span class="cm-link">r</span><span class="cm-link">u</span><span class="cm-link">p</span><span class="cm-link">t</span><span class="cm-link">s</span><span class="cm-link"> </span><span class="cm-link">t</span><span class="cm-link">h</span><span class="cm-link">e</span><span class="cm-link"> </span><span class="cm-link">o</span><span class="cm-link">u</span><span class="cm-link">t</span><span class="cm-link">p</span><span class="cm-link">u</span><span class="cm-link">t</span><span class="cm-link">]</span> |</pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre>For research-specific skills, always include these three regardless of what else you add:</pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre>| Anti-pattern | What it looks like | Why it matters |</pre></div>
<div><pre>|---|---|---|</pre></div>
<div><pre>| <span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">R</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">l</span><span class="cm-strong">e</span><span class="cm-strong"> </span><span class="cm-strong">c</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">f</span><span class="cm-strong">l</span><span class="cm-strong">a</span><span class="cm-strong">t</span><span class="cm-strong">i</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span> | Input refers to &quot;hotel staff&quot; without specifying which role | GM needs ≠ front desk agent needs ≠ night auditor needs — undifferentiated role produces undifferentiated output |</pre></div>
<div><pre>| <span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">S</span><span class="cm-strong">i</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">g</span><span class="cm-strong">l</span><span class="cm-strong">e</span><span class="cm-strong">-</span><span class="cm-strong">q</span><span class="cm-strong">u</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">t</span><span class="cm-strong">e</span><span class="cm-strong"> </span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">p</span><span class="cm-strong">p</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">r</span><span class="cm-strong">t</span><span class="cm-strong">u</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">i</span><span class="cm-strong">t</span><span class="cm-strong">y</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span> | One participant quote used to justify a claim as a pattern | A signal, not a pattern — label the difference explicitly or the output overstates confidence |</pre></div>
<div><pre>| <span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">A</span><span class="cm-strong">s</span><span class="cm-strong">s</span><span class="cm-strong">u</span><span class="cm-strong">m</span><span class="cm-strong">p</span><span class="cm-strong">t</span><span class="cm-strong">i</span><span class="cm-strong">o</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong"> </span><span class="cm-strong">l</span><span class="cm-strong">a</span><span class="cm-strong">u</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">d</span><span class="cm-strong">e</span><span class="cm-strong">r</span><span class="cm-strong">i</span><span class="cm-strong">n</span><span class="cm-strong">g</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span><span class="cm-strong">*</span> | Team intuition presented as a research finding | Intuition is a valid input — label it as such, not as evidence, or the output conflates two different epistemic categories |</pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre><span class="cm-hr">-</span><span class="cm-hr">-</span><span class="cm-hr">-</span></pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>

class="cm-variable-2">d</span><span class="cm-variable-2">y</span></pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
<div><pre>The markers use <span class="cm-link">[</span><span class="cm-link">C</span><span class="cm-link">U</span><span class="cm-link">S</span><span class="cm-link">T</span><span class="cm-link">O</span><span class="cm-link">M</span><span class="cm-link">I</span><span class="cm-link">S</span><span class="cm-link">E</span><span class="cm-link">:</span><span class="cm-link"> </span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">]</span> not placeholder words like &quot;fill&quot; or &quot;TBC&quot; because health_check.py scans for those words and will flag them. <span class="cm-link">[</span><span class="cm-link">C</span><span class="cm-link">U</span><span class="cm-link">S</span><span class="cm-link">T</span><span class="cm-link">O</span><span class="cm-link">M</span><span class="cm-link">I</span><span class="cm-link">S</span><span class="cm-link">E</span><span class="cm-link">:</span><span class="cm-link"> </span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">.</span><span class="cm-link">]</span> is scannable and unambiguous about intent without triggering the check.</pre></div>
<div><pre>&#8203;</pre></div>
